─ Worked for 1m 11s ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• 当前目录是空的，也还不是一个 Git 仓库。我建议这一轮先把项目逻辑定死，再开始落工程骨架；这个项目如果想做到“像真工具、但安装使用很
  轻”，不要做成真 AI 客户端，而要做成一个完全离线的 TUI 模拟器。

  参考方向

  - Codex CLI 给出的信号很明确：终端优先、本地运行、支持全局安装和直接二进制分发，所以我们的产品也应该支持“一条命令安装”和“下载即
    运行”。来源：openai/codex (https://github.com/openai/codex)
  - OpenCode 很强调 TUI、本地 agent 切换，以及前后端解耦，这很适合我们把“界面层”和“伪日志生成器”拆开。来源：anomalyco/opencode
    (https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode)
  - Claude Code 明确支持终端和 Windows 原生安装，说明如果你要“易安装”，Windows 单文件可执行程序应该是第一优先级。来源：Claude Code
    Overview (https://code.claude.com/docs/en/overview)

  我建议的产品定义

  - 本质上不是“AI 编程工具”，而是“终端开发场景模拟器”。
  - 核心目标只有三个：第一眼像真的、完全离线、3 分钟内能装好跑起来。
  - 不要 1:1 复刻品牌 Logo、名称或文案，做成 codex-like、claude-like、opencode-like 三套主题最稳，公开分发时也更安全。

  整体逻辑

  - 屏幕分三层。
  - 顶部区域持续滚动“工具日志”，内容偏系统层，比如扫描目录、索引文件、读取配置、分析 diff、运行测试、网络重试、MCP 工具握手、shell
    调用结果。
  - 中间区域是独立的小说阅读视口，不跟着日志一起跳动，用户可以翻页、换章、搜索、暂停自动滚动。
  - 底部区域持续滚动“代理输出”和“命令回显”，内容偏会话层，比如思考状态、计划步骤、命令执行结果、patch 摘要、token 统计、状态栏。
  - 最底部保留一行拟真的输入提示区，显示当前模式、目录、分支、模型名、审批策略、耗时、token 数等假状态。

  数据流设计

  1. 启动时读取配置文件、主题、小说文件、日志模板。
  2. 生成一个会话 seed，用这个 seed 控制本次“开发任务”的风格，让日志有连续性而不是纯随机。
  3. 伪日志引擎按状态机工作，建议状态为 scan -> plan -> edit -> test -> summarize -> idle 循环。
  4. 每个状态产出两路内容。
  5. 上路写到顶部日志区，偏工具和系统事件。
  6. 下路写到底部日志区，偏 agent 输出和命令回显。
  7. 中间小说区单独维护 viewport，不受上下滚动影响。
  8. 热键可以控制暂停日志、切换主题、切换书籍、跳章、临时显示“任务总结面板”。

  为什么日志不能纯随机

  - 纯随机最容易穿帮。
  - 要做“伪真实”，日志必须有上下文记忆。
  - 比如前面说“发现 package.json”，后面才能出现“install dependencies”。
  - 前面说“running tests”，后面要跟着失败或通过，而不是突然跳到 unrelated 内容。
  - 所以建议做“模板 + 变量 + 状态机 + seed”的生成器，而不是简单定时器刷字符串。

  建议的技术栈

  - 第一选择：Go + Bubble Tea + Lip Gloss + Bubbles
  - 原因很直接：TUI 成熟、跨平台稳定、性能好、最终可以打成单个 exe，用户不需要装 Node。
  - 第二选择才是 Node.js + blessed/neo-blessed
  - 如果你更在意前端开发体验可以选 Node，但“易安装和易分发”不如 Go。

  推荐的项目结构

  moyu-cli/
    cmd/moyu/
    internal/app/
    internal/ui/
    internal/sim/
    internal/content/
    internal/theme/
    internal/config/
    assets/themes/
    assets/log_templates/
    assets/demo_books/
    docs/

  各模块职责

  - ui：三段式终端界面、键盘事件、滚动、状态栏。
  - sim：伪日志状态机、模板渲染、会话 seed、节奏控制。
  - content：导入和切分小说，先支持 .txt，后续再加 .md 和 .epub。
  - theme：配色、边框、标题、状态栏格式，提供三套“类 Codex / 类 Claude / 类 OpenCode”主题。
  - config：首次初始化、默认配置、书籍路径、主题、滚动速度、字体兼容说明。
  - app：把 UI、配置、内容、模拟器组装起来。

  命令设计

  - moyu init
  - moyu run
  - moyu run --theme codex-like --book ./books/xxx.txt
  - moyu import ./novel.txt
  - moyu themes
  这套命令的好处是用户心智低，基本就是“初始化一次，之后直接 run”。

  - 第一阶段直接提供 Windows exe，双击或命令行启动都行。
  - 第二阶段补 scoop 和 winget。
  - 第三阶段再做 macOS/Linux release。
  - 不依赖 API key，不联网也能跑，这一点非常关键，否则安装门槛和故障率都会上去。

  MVP 范围

  - 三段式界面。
  - 一套默认主题，另外两套主题先做皮肤差异。
  - 支持导入 .txt 小说。
  - 上下两路伪日志自动滚动。
  - 支持暂停、换章、切换主题、退出。
  - 支持会话 seed，保证每次运行内容不同但内部自洽。

  第二阶段再做

  - 更丰富的日志模板库。
  - 伪命令执行动画、spinner、进度条。
  - 从当前目录提取真实文件名和项目名，混入日志，进一步增强拟真感。
  - “临时切换为任务摘要/测试面板”的快捷键。
  - 多本小说管理。

  这轮我先没有动文件，因为你明确说要先认真规划。如果这个方向你认可，我下一步就直接在当前目录给你搭一个可运行的 Go 项目骨架，把 moyu
  init、基础三段 TUI 和伪日志引擎第一版一起落出来。

❯ 我就是要假的类似ai在编程的效果而已，不用接真的ai，但是中间呢是我们隐秘的小说文字，像codex他是有高亮和暗淡的输出的，文字部分就可
  以放在暗淡的区域，这样不显眼，然后安装呢我就想直接用pip，然后启动的话，就是直接打开一个cmd窗口，然后输入codenovel就可以打开了，
  然后小说目前先支持从txt文件读取吧

     1 +# codenovel

     3 +`codenovel` is a fake AI coding terminal that hides TXT novel content in a dimmed center pane while synthetic logs scroll a
        bove and below it.
     4 +
     5 +## Install
     6 +
     7 +```bash
     8 +pip install .
     9 +```
    10 +
    11 +For development:
    12 +
    13 +```bash
    14 +pip install -e .
    15 +```
    16 +
    17 +## Run
    18 +
    19 +```bash
    20 +codenovel path/to/novel.txt
    21 +```
    22 +
    23 +Optional flags:
    24 +
    25 +```bash
    26 +codenovel novel.txt --theme codex --title "Sprint Planning"
    27 +```
    28 +
    29 +## Controls
    30 +
    31 +- `j` / `Down`: scroll novel down
    32 +- `k` / `Up`: scroll novel up
    33 +- `PageDown` / `PageUp`: faster scrolling
    34 +- `space`: pause or resume fake logs
    35 +- `t`: cycle themes
    36 +- `q`: quit

     13 +from codenovel.reader import load_book_text, style_book_text

     17 +THEMES = {
     18 +    "codex": {
     19 +        "chrome": "#8fb3ff",
     20 +        "accent": "#d6e4ff",

     48 +BASE_CSS = """
     49 +Screen {
     50 +    background: $background;
     51 +    color: $text;

     53 +
     54 +#root {
     55 +    layout: vertical;
     56 +    height: 1fr;

    101 +    display: none;

    106 +class CodeNovelApp(App[None]):
    107 +    BINDINGS = [
    108 +        Binding("q", "quit", "Quit"),
    109 +        Binding("space", "toggle_pause", "Pause"),
    110 +        Binding("j,down", "scroll_down", "Down"),
    111 +        Binding("k,up", "scroll_up", "Up"),
    112 +        Binding("pagedown", "page_down", "Page Down"),
    113 +        Binding("pageup", "page_up", "Page Up"),
    114 +        Binding("t", "cycle_theme", "Theme"),
    115 +    ]
    116 +
    117 +    paused = reactive(False)
    118 +
    119 +    def __init__(self, book_path: Path | None, theme_name: str, task_title: str) -> None:
    120 +        super().__init__()
    121 +        self.book_path = book_path
    122 +        self.theme_name = theme_name
    123 +        self.task_title = task_title
    124 +        self.theme_order = list(THEMES)
    125 +        self.engine = FakeLogEngine(task_title=task_title, seed=randint(1, 999_999))
    126 +
    127 +    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    128 +        yield Container(
    129 +            RichLog(id="top-pane", classes="pane", wrap=False, highlight=True, markup=True),
    130 +            VerticalScroll(
    131 +                Static(id="reader-text"),
    132 +                id="reader-pane",
    133 +                classes="pane",
    134 +            ),
    135 +            RichLog(id="bottom-pane", classes="pane", wrap=False, highlight=True, markup=True),
    136 +            Static(id="status-line"),
    137 +            id="root",
    138 +        )
    139 +        yield Footer()
    140 +
    141 +    def on_mount(self) -> None:
    142 +        self._apply_theme(self.theme_name)
    143 +        self._load_book()
    144 +        self._seed_logs()
    145 +        self.set_interval(0.38, self._tick_top)
    146 +        self.set_interval(0.58, self._tick_bottom)
    147 +        self._update_status()
    148 +
    149 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    150 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    151 +        styled = style_book_text(book)
    152 +        reader = self.query_one("#reader-text", Static)
    153 +        reader.update(styled)
    154 +
    155 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    156 +        top = self.query_one("#top-pane", RichLog)
    157 +        bottom = self.query_one("#bottom-pane", RichLog)
    158 +        for _ in range(8):
    159 +            top.write(self._render_top(self.engine.next_top_line()))
    160 +        for _ in range(6):
    161 +            bottom.write(self._render_bottom(self.engine.next_bottom_line()))
    162 +
    163 +    def _tick_top(self) -> None:
    164 +        if self.paused:
    165 +            return
    166 +        self.query_one("#top-pane", RichLog).write(
    167 +            self._render_top(self.engine.next_top_line())
    168 +        )
    169 +        self._update_status()
    170 +
    171 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    172 +        if self.paused:
    173 +            return
    174 +        self.query_one("#bottom-pane", RichLog).write(
    175 +            self._render_bottom(self.engine.next_bottom_line())
    176 +        )
    177 +        self._update_status()
    178 +
    179 +    def _render_top(self, line: str) -> Text:
    180 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    181 +        text = Text()
    182 +        text.append("debug ", style=f"bold {palette['chrome']}")
    183 +        text.append(line, style=palette["dim"])
    184 +        return text
    185 +
    186 +    def _render_bottom(self, line: str) -> Text:
    187 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    188 +        text = Text()
    189 +        text.append("assistant ", style=f"bold {palette['accent']}")
    190 +        text.append(line, style=palette["chrome"])
    191 +        return text
    192 +
    193 +    def _update_status(self) -> None:
    194 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    195 +        state = "paused" if self.paused else "streaming"
    196 +        book_name = self.book_path.name if self.book_path else "no-book"
    197 +        line = (
    198 +            f"[{palette['accent']}]model:gpt-5-codex-lite[/]  "
    199 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]mode:auto[/]  "
    200 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]state:{state}[/]  "
    201 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]task:{self.task_title}[/]  "
    202 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]book:{book_name}[/]  "
    203 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]theme:{self.theme_name}[/]"
    204 +        )
    205 +        self.query_one("#status-line", Static).update(line)
    206 +
    207 +    def _apply_theme(self, theme_name: str) -> None:
    208 +        palette = THEMES[theme_name]
    209 +        css = (
    210 +            BASE_CSS.replace("$background", palette["panel"])
    211 +            .replace("$text", palette["accent"])
    212 +            .replace("$accent", palette["chrome"])
    213 +            .replace("$surface", palette["panel"])
    214 +            .replace("$surface_alt", palette["panel_alt"])
    215 +            .replace("$reader", palette["reader"])
    216 +            .replace("$border", palette["border"])
    217 +        )
    218 +        self.theme_name = theme_name
    219 +        self.stylesheet.read(css)
    220 +
    221 +    def action_toggle_pause(self) -> None:
    222 +        self.paused = not self.paused
    223 +        self._update_status()
    224 +
    225 +    def action_scroll_down(self) -> None:
    226 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_down(animate=False)
    227 +
    228 +    def action_scroll_up(self) -> None:
    229 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_up(animate=False)
    230 +
    231 +    def action_page_down(self) -> None:
    232 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_down(animate=False)
    233 +
    234 +    def action_page_up(self) -> None:
    235 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_up(animate=False)
    236 +
    237 +    def action_cycle_theme(self) -> None:
    238 +        current = self.theme_order.index(self.theme_name)
    239 +        next_theme = self.theme_order[(current + 1) % len(self.theme_order)]
    240 +        self._apply_theme(next_theme)
    241 +        self._update_status()

  └ codenovel/reader.py (+42 -0)
     1 +from __future__ import annotations
     2 +
     3 +from pathlib import Path
     4 +
     5 +
     6 +PLACEHOLDER_TEXT = """
     7 +No TXT novel loaded.
     8 +
     9 +Usage:
    10 +  codenovel path\\to\\novel.txt
    11 +
    12 +Tips:
    13 +  - Keep the center pane dim so it reads like inactive terminal output.
    14 +  - Press space to pause logs before turning a page.
    15 +  - Press t to cycle between codex-like, claude-like, and opencode-like themes.
    16 +""".strip()
    17 +
    18 +
    19 +def load_book_text(book_path: Path | None) -> str:
    20 +    if book_path is None:
    21 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    22 +    if not book_path.exists():
    23 +        return f"TXT file not found:\n{book_path}"
    24 +    if book_path.suffix.lower() != ".txt":
    25 +        return f"Only .txt files are supported right now.\n\nProvided:\n{book_path.name}"
    26 +    try:
    27 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    28 +    except UnicodeDecodeError:
    29 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="gb18030", errors="replace")
    30 +
    31 +
    32 +def style_book_text(content: str) -> str:
    33 +    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in content.splitlines()]
    34 +    if not lines:
    35 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    36 +    styled = []
    37 +    for index, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
    38 +        prefix = f"{index:>4} "
    39 +        safe_line = line if line else " "
    40 +        styled.append(f"{prefix}{safe_line}")
    41 +    return "\n".join(styled)

     70 +@dataclass
     71 +class SessionContext:
     72 +    task_title: str
     73 +    seed: int
     74 +    src_count: int = 18
     75 +    test_count: int = 7
     76 +    doc_count: int = 4
     77 +    module_a: str = "terminal/theme.py"
     78 +    module_b: str = "agent/session.py"
     79 +    module_c: str = "reader/pane.py"
     80 +    file_a: str = "src/ui/session_view.tsx"
     81 +    file_b: str = "src/core/runtime.ts"
     82 +    symbol_name: str = "renderSessionState"
     83 +    test_name: str = "tests/test_session_render.py::test_dimmed_reader"
     84 +    latency: int = 34
     85 +    phase_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     86 +    bottom_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     87 +
     88 +    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
     89 +        self.phase_cycle = cycle(TOP_PHASES)
     90 +        self.bottom_cycle = cycle(BOTTOM_PHASES)
     91 +
     92 +
     93 +class FakeLogEngine:
     94 +    def __init__(self, task_title: str, seed: int = 7) -> None:
     95 +        self.random = Random(seed)
     96 +        self.context = SessionContext(task_title=task_title, seed=seed)
     97 +        self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
     98 +        self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
     99 +        self.top_counter = 0
    100 +        self.bottom_counter = 0
    101 +
    102 +    def _render_template(self, template: str) -> str:
    103 +        self.context.src_count += self.random.choice((0, 1))
    104 +        self.context.test_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
    105 +        self.context.doc_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
    106 +        self.context.latency = max(12, self.context.latency + self.random.randint(-4, 7))
    107 +        return template.format(**self.context.__dict__)
    108 +
    109 +    def next_top_line(self) -> str:
    110 +        if self.top_counter and self.top_counter % 4 == 0:
    111 +            self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
    112 +        template = self.random.choice(TOP_TEMPLATES[self.top_phase])
    113 +        self.top_counter += 1
    114 +        return self._render_template(template)
    115 +
    116 +    def next_bottom_line(self) -> str:
    117 +        if self.bottom_counter and self.bottom_counter % 3 == 0:
    118 +            self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
    119 +        template = self.random.choice(BOTTOM_TEMPLATES[self.bottom_phase])
    120 +        self.bottom_counter += 1
    121 +        return self._render_template(template)
    122 +

  └ README.md (+49 -0)
     1 +# codenovel
     2 +
     3 +`codenovel` is a Codex-like fake AI coding terminal that hides TXT novel content in a dimmed center pane while synthetic tr
        anscript activity scrolls around it.
     4 +
     5 +## Install
     6 +
     7 +```bash
     8 +pip install .
     9 +```
    10 +
    11 +For development:
    12 +
    13 +```bash
    14 +pip install -e .
    15 +```
    16 +
    17 +If you open `cmd` in this project directory, you can also run:
    18 +
    19 +```bat
    20 +codenovel novel.txt
    21 +```
    22 +
    23 +The local `codenovel.bat` wrapper calls `python -m codenovel` for you.
    24 +
    25 +## Run
    26 +
    27 +```bash
    28 +codenovel path/to/novel.txt
    29 +```
    30 +
    31 +Equivalent fallback if your `pip` scripts directory is not on `PATH`:
    32 +
    33 +```bash
    34 +python -m codenovel path/to/novel.txt
    35 +```
    36 +
    37 +Optional title override:
    38 +
    39 +```bash
    40 +codenovel novel.txt --title "Summarize recent commits"
    41 +```
    42 +
    43 +## Controls
    44 +
    45 +- `j` / `Down`: scroll novel down
    46 +- `k` / `Up`: scroll novel up
    47 +- `PageDown` / `PageUp`: faster scrolling
    48 +- `space`: pause or resume fake activity
    49 +- `q`: quit

     96 +    def __init__(self, book_path: Path | None, task_title: str) -> None:
     97 +        super().__init__()
     98 +        self.book_path = book_path
     99 +        self.task_title = task_title
    100 +        self.engine = FakeLogEngine(task_title=task_title, seed=randint(1, 999_999))
    101 +        self.started_at = monotonic()
    102 +
    103 +    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    104 +        yield Container(
    105 +            Static(id="header"),
    106 +            RichLog(id="top-log", wrap=True, highlight=False, markup=False),
    107 +            Static(id="reader-label"),
    108 +            VerticalScroll(
    109 +                Static(id="reader-text"),
    110 +                id="reader-scroll",
    111 +            ),
    112 +            RichLog(id="recent-log", wrap=True, highlight=False, markup=False),
    113 +            Static(id="working-line"),
    114 +            Static(id="composer"),
    115 +            Static(id="footer"),
    116 +            id="root",
    117 +        )
    118 +
    119 +    def on_mount(self) -> None:
    120 +        self._render_header()
    121 +        self._load_book()
    122 +        self._render_reader_label()
    123 +        self._render_composer()
    124 +        self._render_footer()
    125 +        self._seed_logs()
    126 +        self._update_working_line()
    127 +        self.set_interval(0.85, self._tick_top)
    128 +        self.set_interval(1.35, self._tick_bottom)
    129 +        self.set_interval(1.0, self._tick_clock)
    130 +
    131 +    def _render_header(self) -> None:
    132 +        model_line = Text()
    133 +        model_line.append("model:     ")
    134 +        model_line.append("gpt-5-codex", style="magenta")
    135 +        model_line.append(" high   ")
    136 +        model_line.append("/model to change", style="dim")
    137 +
    138 +        directory_line = Text()
    139 +        directory_line.append("directory: ")
    140 +        directory_line.append(str(Path.cwd()), style="dim")
    141 +
    142 +        title = Text()
    143 +        title.append(">_ ", style="cyan")
    144 +        title.append("OpenAI Codex", style="bold")
    145 +        title.append(f" (v{__version__})", style="dim")
    146 +
    147 +        header = Text()
    148 +        header.append_text(title)
    149 +        header.append("\n\n")
    150 +        header.append_text(model_line)
    151 +        header.append("\n")
    152 +        header.append_text(directory_line)
    153 +
    154 +        self.query_one("#header", Static).update(Panel.fit(header, border_style="white"))
    155 +
    156 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    157 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    158 +        self.query_one("#reader-text", Static).update(style_book_text(book))
    159 +
    160 +    def _render_reader_label(self) -> None:
    161 +        self.query_one("#reader-label", Static).update(
    162 +            Text("  inactive terminal output", style="dim")
    163 +        )
    164 +
    165 +    def _render_composer(self) -> None:
    166 +        composer = Text()
    167 +        composer.append("\n")
    168 +        composer.append("› ", style="magenta")
    169 +        composer.append("Ask Codex to do anything")
    170 +        composer.append("\n")
    171 +        self.query_one("#composer", Static).update(composer)
    172 +
    173 +    def _render_footer(self) -> None:
    174 +        width = max(self.size.width - 38, 1)
    175 +        footer = Text()
    176 +        footer.append("  ")
    177 +        footer.append("?", style="cyan")
    178 +        footer.append(" for shortcuts", style="dim")
    179 +        footer.append(" " * width)
    180 +        footer.append("100% context left", style="dim")
    181 +        self.query_one("#footer", Static).update(footer)
    182 +
    183 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    184 +        top = self.query_one("#top-log", RichLog)
    185 +        recent = self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog)
    186 +        recent.write(self._render_user_prompt(self.engine.initial_prompt()))
    187 +        for _ in range(5):
    188 +            self._write_group(top, self.engine.next_top_group())
    189 +        for _ in range(2):
    190 +            self._write_group(recent, self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    191 +
    192 +    def _tick_top(self) -> None:
    193 +        if self.paused:
    194 +            return
    195 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#top-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_top_group())
    196 +        self._update_working_line()
    197 +
    198 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    199 +        if self.paused:
    200 +            return
    201 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    202 +        self._update_working_line()
    203 +
    204 +    def _tick_clock(self) -> None:
    205 +        self._update_working_line()
    206 +        self._render_footer()
    207 +
    208 +    def _update_working_line(self) -> None:
    209 +        elapsed = int(monotonic() - self.started_at)
    210 +        line = Text()
    211 +        line.append("• ", style="magenta")
    212 +        line.append(self.engine.working_status(elapsed, self.paused))
    213 +        self.query_one("#working-line", Static).update(line)
    214 +
    215 +    def _write_group(self, widget: RichLog, lines: list[RenderedLine]) -> None:
    216 +        for line in lines:
    217 +            widget.write(self._render_line(line))
    218 +
    219 +    def _render_user_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> Text:
    220 +        line = Text()
    221 +        line.append("› ", style="magenta")
    222 +        line.append(prompt)
    223 +        return line
    224 +
    225 +    def _render_line(self, line: RenderedLine) -> Text:
    226 +        text = Text()
    227 +        if line.kind == "commentary":
    228 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    229 +            text.append(line.text)
    230 +        elif line.kind == "event":
    231 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    232 +            text.append(line.text)
    233 +        elif line.kind == "child":
    234 +            text.append("  └ ", style="dim")
    235 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    236 +        elif line.kind == "child_deep":
    237 +            text.append("    ")
    238 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    239 +        elif line.kind == "command":
    240 +            text.append("  ")
    241 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    242 +        elif line.kind == "success":
    243 +            text.append("    ")
    244 +            text.append(line.text, style="green")
    245 +        elif line.kind == "queue":
    246 +            text.append("  → ", style="dim")
    247 +            text.append(line.text)
    248 +        elif line.kind == "summary":
    249 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    250 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    251 +        else:
    252 +            text.append(line.text)
    253 +        return text
    254 +
    255 +    def action_toggle_pause(self) -> None:
    256 +        self.paused = not self.paused
    257 +        self._update_working_line()
    258 +
    259 +    def action_scroll_down(self) -> None:
    260 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_down(animate=False)
    261 +
    262 +    def action_scroll_up(self) -> None:
    263 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_up(animate=False)
    264 +
    265 +    def action_page_down(self) -> None:
    266 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_down(animate=False)
    267 +
    268 +    def action_page_up(self) -> None:
    269 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_up(animate=False)

  └ codenovel/reader.py (+36 -0)
     1 +from __future__ import annotations
     2 +
     3 +from pathlib import Path
     4 +
     5 +
     6 +PLACEHOLDER_TEXT = """
     7 +No TXT novel loaded.
     8 +
     9 +Usage:
    10 +  codenovel path\\to\\novel.txt
    11 +
    12 +Tips:
    13 +  - The center pane is intentionally dim so it reads like inactive terminal output.
    14 +  - Press space to pause the fake activity before turning a page.
    15 +  - Press j/k or PageDown/PageUp to move through the TXT file.
    16 +""".strip()
    17 +
    18 +
    19 +def load_book_text(book_path: Path | None) -> str:
    20 +    if book_path is None:
    21 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    22 +    if not book_path.exists():
    23 +        return f"TXT file not found:\n{book_path}"
    24 +    if book_path.suffix.lower() != ".txt":
    25 +        return f"Only .txt files are supported right now.\n\nProvided:\n{book_path.name}"
    26 +    try:
    27 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    28 +    except UnicodeDecodeError:
    29 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="gb18030", errors="replace")
    30 +
    31 +
    32 +def style_book_text(content: str) -> str:
    33 +    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in content.splitlines()]
    34 +    if not lines:
    35 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    36 +    return "\n".join(f"  {line if line else ' '}" for line in lines)

  └ codenovel/simulator.py (+197 -0)
      1 +from __future__ import annotations
      2 +
      3 +from dataclasses import dataclass, field
      4 +from itertools import cycle
      5 +from random import Random
      6 +
      7 +
      8 +TOP_PHASES = ("commentary", "explore", "inspect", "edit", "test", "summarize")
      9 +BOTTOM_PHASES = ("follow_up", "command", "summary")
     10 +
     11 +
     12 +@dataclass(frozen=True)
     13 +class RenderedLine:
     14 +    kind: str
     15 +    text: str
     16 +
     17 +
     18 +@dataclass
     19 +class SessionContext:
     20 +    task_title: str
     21 +    seed: int
     22 +    src_count: int = 18
     23 +    test_count: int = 7
     24 +    doc_count: int = 4
     25 +    module_a: str = "tui/src/bottom_pane/footer.rs"
     26 +    module_b: str = "tui/src/chatwidget.rs"
     27 +    module_c: str = "tui/src/history_cell.rs"
     28 +    file_a: str = "tui/src/app.rs"
     29 +    file_b: str = "tui/src/bottom_pane/chat_composer.rs"
     30 +    symbol_name: str = "render_status_footer"
     31 +    test_name: str = "tests/test_session_render.py::test_dimmed_reader"
     32 +    latency: int = 34
     33 +    phase_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     34 +    bottom_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     35 +
     36 +    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
     37 +        self.phase_cycle = cycle(TOP_PHASES)
     38 +        self.bottom_cycle = cycle(BOTTOM_PHASES)
     39 +
     40 +
     41 +class FakeLogEngine:
     42 +    def __init__(self, task_title: str, seed: int = 7) -> None:
     43 +        self.random = Random(seed)
     44 +        self.context = SessionContext(task_title=task_title, seed=seed)
     45 +        self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
     46 +        self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
     47 +        self.top_counter = 0
     48 +        self.bottom_counter = 0
     49 +
     50 +    def _render_template(self, template: str) -> str:
     51 +        self.context.src_count += self.random.choice((0, 1))
     52 +        self.context.test_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
     53 +        self.context.doc_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
     54 +        self.context.latency = max(12, self.context.latency + self.random.randint(-4, 7))
     55 +        return template.format(**self.context.__dict__)
     56 +
     57 +    def initial_prompt(self) -> str:
     58 +        return self.context.task_title
     59 +
     60 +    def working_status(self, elapsed_seconds: int, paused: bool) -> str:
     61 +        if paused:
     62 +            return f"Paused ({elapsed_seconds}s • q to quit)"
     63 +
     64 +        phase_map = {
     65 +            "commentary": "Thinking through the next change",
     66 +            "explore": "Exploring the codebase",
     67 +            "inspect": "Investigating rendering code",
     68 +            "edit": "Editing the current approach",
     69 +            "test": "Running validation checks",
     70 +            "summarize": "Summarizing recent progress",
     71 +        }
     72 +        label = phase_map.get(self.top_phase, "Working")
     73 +        return f"{label} ({elapsed_seconds}s • esc to interrupt)"
     74 +
     75 +    def next_top_group(self) -> list[RenderedLine]:
     76 +        if self.top_counter and self.top_counter % 4 == 0:
     77 +            self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
     78 +        self.top_counter += 1
     79 +
     80 +        if self.top_phase == "commentary":
     81 +            template = self.random.choice(
     82 +                [
     83 +                    "I'm going to inspect the rendering path around {symbol_name} before changing anything.",
     84 +                    "I want to confirm where the current session UI is composing history cells and status rows.",
     85 +                    "I'm tracing how '{task_title}' should read in the terminal before touching the fake transcript.",
     86 +                ]
     87 +            )
     88 +            return [RenderedLine("commentary", self._render_template(template))]
     89 +
     90 +        if self.top_phase == "explore":
     91 +            search = self.random.choice(
     92 +                [
     93 +                    "Search status footer layout",
     94 +                    "Search queued message rendering",
     95 +                    "Search transcript viewport",
     96 +                    "Search terminal title update",
     97 +                ]
     98 +            )
     99 +            read_target = self.random.choice(
    100 +                [
    101 +                    self.context.module_a,
    102 +                    self.context.module_b,
    103 +                    self.context.module_c,
    104 +                    self.context.file_a,
    105 +                ]
    106 +            )
    107 +            return [
    108 +                RenderedLine("event", "Explored"),
    109 +                RenderedLine("child", search),
    110 +                RenderedLine("child_deep", f"Read {read_target}"),
    111 +            ]
    112 +
    113 +        if self.top_phase == "inspect":
    114 +            template = self.random.choice(
    115 +                [
    116 +                    "Inspecting how dim secondary text is rendered in long-running sessions.",
    117 +                    "Checking whether the working indicator and footer collapse conflict at narrow widths.",
    118 +                    "Reviewing how file reads and status hints are grouped together in the transcript.",
    119 +                ]
    120 +            )
    121 +            return [RenderedLine("event", self._render_template(template))]
    122 +
    123 +        if self.top_phase == "edit":
    124 +            template = self.random.choice(
    125 +                [
    126 +                    "Preparing a narrow UI rewrite around {file_a}.",
    127 +                    "Adjusting the current transcript structure so the hidden reader stays inconspicuous.",
    128 +                    "Keeping the fake session noisy enough to mask a long central output block.",
    129 +                ]
    130 +            )
    131 +            return [RenderedLine("event", self._render_template(template))]
    132 +
    133 +        if self.top_phase == "test":
    134 +            command = self.random.choice(
    135 +                [
    136 +                    "$ pytest tests/test_session_render.py -q",
    137 +                    "$ rg -n \"context left\" tui/src",
    138 +                    "$ python -m build",
    139 +                    "$ git diff --stat",
    140 +                ]
    141 +            )
    142 +            result = self.random.choice(
    143 +                [
    144 +                    "1 passed in 0.34s",
    145 +                    "render path confirmed",
    146 +                    f"p95={self.context.latency}ms",
    147 +                    "no unexpected regressions",
    148 +                ]
    149 +            )
    150 +            return [
    151 +                RenderedLine("event", "Ran validation"),
    152 +                RenderedLine("command", command),
    153 +                RenderedLine("success", result),
    154 +            ]
    155 +
    156 +        template = self.random.choice(
    157 +            [
    158 +                "Summarizing the current pass before the next synthetic turn.",
    159 +                "The layout is converging on a more transcript-first terminal shape.",
    160 +                "Recent edits are keeping the output calm while the center block stays dim.",
    161 +            ]
    162 +        )
    163 +        return [RenderedLine("summary", self._render_template(template))]
    164 +
    165 +    def next_bottom_group(self) -> list[RenderedLine]:
    166 +        if self.bottom_counter and self.bottom_counter % 3 == 0:
    167 +            self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
    168 +        self.bottom_counter += 1
    169 +
    170 +        if self.bottom_phase == "follow_up":
    171 +            return [
    172 +                RenderedLine("event", "Queued follow-up messages"),
    173 +                RenderedLine("queue", self.context.task_title),
    174 +            ]
    175 +
    176 +        if self.bottom_phase == "command":
    177 +            command = self.random.choice(
    178 +                [
    179 +                    f"$ rg -n \"{self.context.symbol_name}\" {self.context.file_a}",
    180 +                    f"$ sed -n '1,140p' {self.context.file_b}",

    182 +                    "$ git status --short",
    183 +                ]
    184 +            )

    187 +                RenderedLine("child_deep", "capturing output for transcript"),
    188 +            ]
    189 +
    190 +        summary = self.random.choice(
    191 +            [
    192 +                "Recent checks look stable enough for another pass.",
    193 +                "The fake activity stream is staying coherent across the last few updates.",
    194 +                "Current output density is close to the real Codex CLI pacing.",
    195 +            ]
    196 +        )
    197 +        return [RenderedLine("summary", summary)]

     87 +class CodeNovelApp(App[None]):
     88 +    CSS = BASE_CSS
     89 +    BINDINGS = [
     90 +        Binding("q", "quit", "Quit"),
     91 +        Binding("space", "toggle_pause", "Pause"),
     92 +        Binding("j,down", "scroll_down", "Down"),
     93 +        Binding("k,up", "scroll_up", "Up"),
     94 +        Binding("pagedown", "page_down", "Page Down"),
     95 +        Binding("pageup", "page_up", "Page Up"),
     96 +    ]
     97 +
     98 +    paused = reactive(False)
     99 +
    100 +    def __init__(self, book_path: Path | None, task_title: str) -> None:
    101 +        super().__init__()
    102 +        self.book_path = book_path
    103 +        self.task_title = task_title
    104 +        self.engine = FakeLogEngine(task_title=task_title, seed=randint(1, 999_999))
    105 +        self.started_at = monotonic()
    106 +        self.book_lines: list[str] = []
    107 +        self.book_offset = 0
    108 +
    109 +    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    110 +        yield VerticalScroll(
    111 +            Container(
    112 +                Static(id="transcript"),
    113 +                Static(id="reader-label"),
    114 +                Static(id="reader-text"),
    115 +                RichLog(id="recent-log", wrap=True, highlight=False, markup=False),
    116 +                Static(id="working-line"),
    117 +                Static(id="composer"),
    118 +                Static(id="status-compact"),
    119 +                Static(id="status-detail"),
    120 +                id="root",
    121 +            ),
    122 +            id="app-scroll",
    123 +        )
    124 +
    125 +    def on_mount(self) -> None:
    126 +        self._render_transcript()
    127 +        self._load_book()
    128 +        self._render_reader_label()
    129 +        self._render_composer()
    130 +        self._hide_scrollbars()
    131 +        self._render_status_lines()
    132 +        self._seed_logs()
    133 +        self._update_working_line()
    134 +        self.set_interval(1.35, self._tick_bottom)
    135 +        self.set_interval(1.0, self._tick_clock)
    136 +
    137 +    def _render_transcript(self) -> None:
    138 +        preview = Text()
    139 +        for index, line in enumerate(self.engine.transcript_preview()):
    140 +            if index:
    141 +                preview.append("\n")
    142 +            preview.append_text(self._render_line(line))
    143 +        self.query_one("#transcript", Static).update(preview)
    144 +
    145 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    146 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    147 +        self.book_lines = split_book_lines(book)
    148 +        self.book_offset = 0
    149 +        self._render_book_view()
    150 +
    151 +    def _render_book_view(self) -> None:
    152 +        total_lines = len(self.book_lines)
    153 +        max_offset = max(total_lines - 4, 0)
    154 +        self.book_offset = max(0, min(self.book_offset, max_offset))
    155 +        visible = self.book_lines[self.book_offset : self.book_offset + 4]
    156 +        while len(visible) < 4:
    157 +            visible.append("  ")
    158 +        self.query_one("#reader-text", Static).update("\n".join(visible))
    159 +
    160 +    def _render_reader_label(self) -> None:
    161 +        self.query_one("#reader-label", Static).update(
    162 +            Text("  inactive terminal output", style="dim")
    163 +        )
    164 +
    165 +    def _render_composer(self) -> None:
    166 +        composer = Text()
    167 +        composer.append("\n")
    168 +        composer.append("› ", style="magenta")
    169 +        composer.append("Ask Codex to do anything")
    170 +        composer.append("\n")
    171 +        self.query_one("#composer", Static).update(composer)
    172 +
    173 +    def _hide_scrollbars(self) -> None:
    174 +        self.query_one("#app-scroll", VerticalScroll).show_vertical_scrollbar = False
    175 +        self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog).show_vertical_scrollbar = False
    176 +
    177 +    def _render_status_lines(self) -> None:
    178 +        cwd = Path.cwd()
    179 +        project_name = cwd.name or "workspace"
    180 +
    181 +        compact = Text()
    182 +        compact.append("   ", style="cyan")
    183 +        compact.append("GPT 5.4 ·hi", style="white")
    184 +        compact.append(" │ ", style="dim")
    185 +        compact.append(project_name, style="white")
    186 +        compact.append(" │ ", style="dim")
    187 +        compact.append(" ", style="magenta")
    188 +        compact.append("61% left · 108.4k tokens", style="white")
    189 +        self.query_one("#status-compact", Static).update(compact)
    190 +
    191 +        detail = Text()
    192 +        detail.append("  gpt-5.4 high", style="white")
    193 +        detail.append(" · ", style="dim")
    194 +        detail.append("61% left", style="white")
    195 +        detail.append(" · ", style="dim")
    196 +        detail.append(str(cwd), style="#a6a6a6")
    197 +        self.query_one("#status-detail", Static).update(detail)
    198 +
    199 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    200 +        recent = self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog)
    201 +        recent.write(self._render_user_prompt(self.engine.initial_prompt()))
    202 +        for _ in range(2):
    203 +            self._write_group(recent, self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    204 +
    205 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    206 +        if self.paused:
    207 +            return
    208 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    209 +        self._update_working_line()
    210 +
    211 +    def _tick_clock(self) -> None:
    212 +        self._update_working_line()
    213 +        self._render_status_lines()
    214 +
    215 +    def _update_working_line(self) -> None:
    216 +        elapsed = int(monotonic() - self.started_at)
    217 +        line = Text()
    218 +        line.append("• ", style="magenta")
    219 +        line.append(self.engine.working_status(elapsed, self.paused))
    220 +        self.query_one("#working-line", Static).update(line)
    221 +
    222 +    def _write_group(self, widget: RichLog, lines: list[RenderedLine]) -> None:
    223 +        for line in lines:
    224 +            widget.write(self._render_line(line))
    225 +
    226 +    def _render_user_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> Text:
    227 +        line = Text()
    228 +        line.append("› ", style="magenta")
    229 +        line.append(prompt)
    230 +        return line
    231 +
    232 +    def _render_line(self, line: RenderedLine) -> Text:
    233 +        text = Text()
    234 +        if line.kind in {"commentary", "event"}:
    235 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    236 +            text.append(line.text)
    237 +        elif line.kind == "child":
    238 +            text.append("  └ ", style="dim")
    239 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    240 +        elif line.kind == "child_deep":
    241 +            text.append("    ")
    242 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    243 +        elif line.kind == "command":
    244 +            text.append("  ")
    245 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    246 +        elif line.kind == "success":
    247 +            text.append("    ")

    126 +        self._render_transcript()
    127 +        self._load_book()

    138 +        preview = Text()
    139 +        for index, line in enumerate(self.engine.transcript_preview()):
    140 +            if index:
    141 +                preview.append("\n")
    142 +            preview.append_text(self._render_line(line))
    143 +        self.query_one("#transcript", Static).update(preview)

    145 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    146 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    147 +        self.book_lines = split_book_lines(book)
    148 +        self.book_offset = 0
    149 +        self._render_book_view()
    150 +
    151 +    def _render_book_view(self) -> None:
    152 +        total_lines = len(self.book_lines)
    153 +        max_offset = max(total_lines - 4, 0)
    154 +        self.book_offset = max(0, min(self.book_offset, max_offset))
    155 +        visible = self.book_lines[self.book_offset : self.book_offset + 4]
    156 +        while len(visible) < 4:
    157 +            visible.append("  ")
    158 +        self.query_one("#reader-text", Static).update("\n".join(visible))
    159 +

    164 +

    175 +        self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog).show_vertical_scrollbar = False

    198 +
    199 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    200 +        recent = self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog)
    201 +        recent.write(self._render_user_prompt(self.engine.initial_prompt()))
    202 +        for _ in range(2):
    203 +            self._write_group(recent, self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    204 +
    205 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    206 +        if self.paused:
    207 +            return
    208 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    209 +        self._update_working_line()
    210 +
    211 +    def _tick_clock(self) -> None:
    212 +        self._update_working_line()
    213 +        self._render_status_lines()
    214 +
    215 +    def _update_working_line(self) -> None:
    216 +        elapsed = int(monotonic() - self.started_at)
    217 +        line = Text()
    218 +        line.append("• ", style="magenta")
    219 +        line.append(self.engine.working_status(elapsed, self.paused))
    220 +        self.query_one("#working-line", Static).update(line)
    221 +
    222 +    def _write_group(self, widget: RichLog, lines: list[RenderedLine]) -> None:
    223 +        for line in lines:
    224 +            widget.write(self._render_line(line))
    225 +
    226 +    def _render_user_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> Text:
    227 +        line = Text()
    228 +        line.append("› ", style="magenta")
    229 +        line.append(prompt)
    230 +        return line
    231 +
    232 +    def _render_line(self, line: RenderedLine) -> Text:
    233 +        text = Text()
    234 +        if line.kind in {"commentary", "event"}:
    235 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    236 +            text.append(line.text)
    237 +        elif line.kind == "child":
    238 +            text.append("  └ ", style="dim")
    239 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    240 +        elif line.kind == "child_deep":
    241 +            text.append("    ")
    242 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    243 +        elif line.kind == "command":
    244 +            text.append("  ")
    245 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    246 +        elif line.kind == "success":
    247 +            text.append("    ")
    248 +            text.append(line.text, style="green")
    249 +        elif line.kind == "queue":
    250 +            text.append("  → ", style="dim")
    251 +            text.append(line.text)
    252 +        elif line.kind == "summary":
    253 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    254 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    255 +        else:
    256 +            text.append(line.text)
    257 +        return text
    258 +
    259 +    def action_toggle_pause(self) -> None:
    260 +        self.paused = not self.paused
    261 +        self._update_working_line()

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• 这个项目本质上是个“伪装成 AI 编码终端的 TXT 小说阅读器”，不是一个真正的 AI 编程工具。README 直接写了它是
  “Codex-like fake AI coding terminal”，把小说内容藏在中间一块偏暗的区域，周围滚动假的开发日志和状态信息。
  README.md:1 README.md:3

  从代码看，实际入口很简单：命令行接受一个 book 路径和一个可选的 --title，然后启动 CodeNovelApp 这个 Textual 终
  端 UI。codenovel/cli.py:9 codenovel/cli.py:28

  核心结构是这样：

  - 界面层在 codenovel/ui_app.py:127，用 textual/rich 画出一个黑底终端界面。
  - 中间只显示 4 行真实小说内容，并支持 j/k、方向键、PageUp/PageDown 翻页。codenovel/ui_app.py:19 codenovel/
    ui_app.py:198 README.md:43
  - 假日志是 codenovel/simulator.py:41 里随机生成的，会伪造 Explored、Ran validation、Applied patch、warning、
    diff 之类的输出。
  - 读书逻辑在 codenovel/reader.py:19，只支持 .txt，优先按 UTF-8 读取，失败就回退到 gb18030，明显是考虑中 文小说
    文本。codenovel/reader.py:24 codenovel/reader.py:26

  你可以把它理解成一个“摸鱼工具”：

  - 表面上像在用 Codex/CLI 写代码
  - 实际上中间在看 TXT 小说
  - space 可以暂停假的活动流，方便翻页

  另外，仓库里的 _reference_codex/ 不是这个程序的主逻辑，更像是拿来参考真实 Codex 项目结构和界面风格的资料目录；
  真正跑起来的是 codenovel/ 这个包。还有一个细节是 codenovel/app.py 看起来像早期版本，当前 CLI 实际引用的是
  codenovel/ui_app.py。
─ Worked for 1m 11s ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

• 当前目录是空的，也还不是一个 Git 仓库。我建议这一轮先把项目逻辑定死，再开始落工程骨架；这个项目如果想做到“像真工具、但安装使用很
  轻”，不要做成真 AI 客户端，而要做成一个完全离线的 TUI 模拟器。

  参考方向

  - Codex CLI 给出的信号很明确：终端优先、本地运行、支持全局安装和直接二进制分发，所以我们的产品也应该支持“一条命令安装”和“下载即
    运行”。来源：openai/codex (https://github.com/openai/codex)
  - OpenCode 很强调 TUI、本地 agent 切换，以及前后端解耦，这很适合我们把“界面层”和“伪日志生成器”拆开。来源：anomalyco/opencode
    (https://github.com/anomalyco/opencode)
  - Claude Code 明确支持终端和 Windows 原生安装，说明如果你要“易安装”，Windows 单文件可执行程序应该是第一优先级。来源：Claude Code
    Overview (https://code.claude.com/docs/en/overview)

  我建议的产品定义

  - 本质上不是“AI 编程工具”，而是“终端开发场景模拟器”。
  - 核心目标只有三个：第一眼像真的、完全离线、3 分钟内能装好跑起来。
  - 不要 1:1 复刻品牌 Logo、名称或文案，做成 codex-like、claude-like、opencode-like 三套主题最稳，公开分发时也更安全。

  整体逻辑

  - 屏幕分三层。
  - 顶部区域持续滚动“工具日志”，内容偏系统层，比如扫描目录、索引文件、读取配置、分析 diff、运行测试、网络重试、MCP 工具握手、shell
    调用结果。
  - 中间区域是独立的小说阅读视口，不跟着日志一起跳动，用户可以翻页、换章、搜索、暂停自动滚动。
  - 底部区域持续滚动“代理输出”和“命令回显”，内容偏会话层，比如思考状态、计划步骤、命令执行结果、patch 摘要、token 统计、状态栏。
  - 最底部保留一行拟真的输入提示区，显示当前模式、目录、分支、模型名、审批策略、耗时、token 数等假状态。

  数据流设计

  1. 启动时读取配置文件、主题、小说文件、日志模板。
  2. 生成一个会话 seed，用这个 seed 控制本次“开发任务”的风格，让日志有连续性而不是纯随机。
  3. 伪日志引擎按状态机工作，建议状态为 scan -> plan -> edit -> test -> summarize -> idle 循环。
  4. 每个状态产出两路内容。
  5. 上路写到顶部日志区，偏工具和系统事件。
  6. 下路写到底部日志区，偏 agent 输出和命令回显。
  7. 中间小说区单独维护 viewport，不受上下滚动影响。
  8. 热键可以控制暂停日志、切换主题、切换书籍、跳章、临时显示“任务总结面板”。

  为什么日志不能纯随机

  - 纯随机最容易穿帮。
  - 要做“伪真实”，日志必须有上下文记忆。
  - 比如前面说“发现 package.json”，后面才能出现“install dependencies”。
  - 前面说“running tests”，后面要跟着失败或通过，而不是突然跳到 unrelated 内容。
  - 所以建议做“模板 + 变量 + 状态机 + seed”的生成器，而不是简单定时器刷字符串。

  建议的技术栈

  - 第一选择：Go + Bubble Tea + Lip Gloss + Bubbles
  - 原因很直接：TUI 成熟、跨平台稳定、性能好、最终可以打成单个 exe，用户不需要装 Node。
  - 第二选择才是 Node.js + blessed/neo-blessed
  - 如果你更在意前端开发体验可以选 Node，但“易安装和易分发”不如 Go。

  推荐的项目结构

  moyu-cli/
    cmd/moyu/
    internal/app/
    internal/ui/
    internal/sim/
    internal/content/
    internal/theme/
    internal/config/
    assets/themes/
    assets/log_templates/
    assets/demo_books/
    docs/

  各模块职责

  - ui：三段式终端界面、键盘事件、滚动、状态栏。
  - sim：伪日志状态机、模板渲染、会话 seed、节奏控制。
  - content：导入和切分小说，先支持 .txt，后续再加 .md 和 .epub。
  - theme：配色、边框、标题、状态栏格式，提供三套“类 Codex / 类 Claude / 类 OpenCode”主题。
  - config：首次初始化、默认配置、书籍路径、主题、滚动速度、字体兼容说明。
  - app：把 UI、配置、内容、模拟器组装起来。

  命令设计

  - moyu init
  - moyu run
  - moyu run --theme codex-like --book ./books/xxx.txt
  - moyu import ./novel.txt
  - moyu themes
  这套命令的好处是用户心智低，基本就是“初始化一次，之后直接 run”。

  - 第一阶段直接提供 Windows exe，双击或命令行启动都行。
  - 第二阶段补 scoop 和 winget。
  - 第三阶段再做 macOS/Linux release。
  - 不依赖 API key，不联网也能跑，这一点非常关键，否则安装门槛和故障率都会上去。

  MVP 范围

  - 三段式界面。
  - 一套默认主题，另外两套主题先做皮肤差异。
  - 支持导入 .txt 小说。
  - 上下两路伪日志自动滚动。
  - 支持暂停、换章、切换主题、退出。
  - 支持会话 seed，保证每次运行内容不同但内部自洽。

  第二阶段再做

  - 更丰富的日志模板库。
  - 伪命令执行动画、spinner、进度条。
  - 从当前目录提取真实文件名和项目名，混入日志，进一步增强拟真感。
  - “临时切换为任务摘要/测试面板”的快捷键。
  - 多本小说管理。

  这轮我先没有动文件，因为你明确说要先认真规划。如果这个方向你认可，我下一步就直接在当前目录给你搭一个可运行的 Go 项目骨架，把 moyu
  init、基础三段 TUI 和伪日志引擎第一版一起落出来。

❯ 我就是要假的类似ai在编程的效果而已，不用接真的ai，但是中间呢是我们隐秘的小说文字，像codex他是有高亮和暗淡的输出的，文字部分就可
  以放在暗淡的区域，这样不显眼，然后安装呢我就想直接用pip，然后启动的话，就是直接打开一个cmd窗口，然后输入codenovel就可以打开了，
  然后小说目前先支持从txt文件读取吧

    106 +class CodeNovelApp(App[None]):
    107 +    BINDINGS = [
    108 +        Binding("q", "quit", "Quit"),
    109 +        Binding("space", "toggle_pause", "Pause"),
    110 +        Binding("j,down", "scroll_down", "Down"),
    111 +        Binding("k,up", "scroll_up", "Up"),
    112 +        Binding("pagedown", "page_down", "Page Down"),
    113 +        Binding("pageup", "page_up", "Page Up"),
    114 +        Binding("t", "cycle_theme", "Theme"),
    115 +    ]
    116 +
    117 +    paused = reactive(False)
    118 +
    119 +    def __init__(self, book_path: Path | None, theme_name: str, task_title: str) -> None:
    120 +        super().__init__()
    121 +        self.book_path = book_path
    122 +        self.theme_name = theme_name
    123 +        self.task_title = task_title
    124 +        self.theme_order = list(THEMES)
    125 +        self.engine = FakeLogEngine(task_title=task_title, seed=randint(1, 999_999))
    126 +
    127 +    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    128 +        yield Container(
    129 +            RichLog(id="top-pane", classes="pane", wrap=False, highlight=True, markup=True),
    130 +            VerticalScroll(
    131 +                Static(id="reader-text"),
    132 +                id="reader-pane",
    133 +                classes="pane",
    134 +            ),
    135 +            RichLog(id="bottom-pane", classes="pane", wrap=False, highlight=True, markup=True),
    136 +            Static(id="status-line"),
    137 +            id="root",
    138 +        )
    139 +        yield Footer()
    140 +
    141 +    def on_mount(self) -> None:
    142 +        self._apply_theme(self.theme_name)
    143 +        self._load_book()
    144 +        self._seed_logs()
    145 +        self.set_interval(0.38, self._tick_top)
    146 +        self.set_interval(0.58, self._tick_bottom)
    147 +        self._update_status()
    148 +
    149 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    150 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    151 +        styled = style_book_text(book)
    152 +        reader = self.query_one("#reader-text", Static)
    153 +        reader.update(styled)
    154 +
    155 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    156 +        top = self.query_one("#top-pane", RichLog)
    157 +        bottom = self.query_one("#bottom-pane", RichLog)
    158 +        for _ in range(8):
    159 +            top.write(self._render_top(self.engine.next_top_line()))
    160 +        for _ in range(6):
    161 +            bottom.write(self._render_bottom(self.engine.next_bottom_line()))
    162 +
    163 +    def _tick_top(self) -> None:
    164 +        if self.paused:
    165 +            return
    166 +        self.query_one("#top-pane", RichLog).write(
    167 +            self._render_top(self.engine.next_top_line())
    168 +        )
    169 +        self._update_status()
    170 +
    171 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    172 +        if self.paused:
    173 +            return
    174 +        self.query_one("#bottom-pane", RichLog).write(
    175 +            self._render_bottom(self.engine.next_bottom_line())
    176 +        )
    177 +        self._update_status()
    178 +
    179 +    def _render_top(self, line: str) -> Text:
    180 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    181 +        text = Text()
    182 +        text.append("debug ", style=f"bold {palette['chrome']}")
    183 +        text.append(line, style=palette["dim"])
    184 +        return text
    185 +
    186 +    def _render_bottom(self, line: str) -> Text:
    187 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    188 +        text = Text()
    189 +        text.append("assistant ", style=f"bold {palette['accent']}")
    190 +        text.append(line, style=palette["chrome"])
    191 +        return text
    192 +
    193 +    def _update_status(self) -> None:
    194 +        palette = THEMES[self.theme_name]
    195 +        state = "paused" if self.paused else "streaming"
    196 +        book_name = self.book_path.name if self.book_path else "no-book"
    197 +        line = (
    198 +            f"[{palette['accent']}]model:gpt-5-codex-lite[/]  "
    199 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]mode:auto[/]  "
    200 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]state:{state}[/]  "
    201 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]task:{self.task_title}[/]  "
    202 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]book:{book_name}[/]  "
    203 +            f"[{palette['chrome']}]theme:{self.theme_name}[/]"
    204 +        )
    205 +        self.query_one("#status-line", Static).update(line)
    206 +
    207 +    def _apply_theme(self, theme_name: str) -> None:
    208 +        palette = THEMES[theme_name]
    209 +        css = (
    210 +            BASE_CSS.replace("$background", palette["panel"])
    211 +            .replace("$text", palette["accent"])
    212 +            .replace("$accent", palette["chrome"])
    213 +            .replace("$surface", palette["panel"])
    214 +            .replace("$surface_alt", palette["panel_alt"])
    215 +            .replace("$reader", palette["reader"])
    216 +            .replace("$border", palette["border"])
    217 +        )
    218 +        self.theme_name = theme_name
    219 +        self.stylesheet.read(css)
    220 +
    221 +    def action_toggle_pause(self) -> None:
    222 +        self.paused = not self.paused
    223 +        self._update_status()
    224 +
    225 +    def action_scroll_down(self) -> None:
    226 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_down(animate=False)
    227 +
    228 +    def action_scroll_up(self) -> None:
    229 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_up(animate=False)
    230 +
    231 +    def action_page_down(self) -> None:
    232 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_down(animate=False)
    233 +
    234 +    def action_page_up(self) -> None:
    235 +        self.query_one("#reader-pane", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_up(animate=False)
    236 +
    237 +    def action_cycle_theme(self) -> None:
    238 +        current = self.theme_order.index(self.theme_name)
    239 +        next_theme = self.theme_order[(current + 1) % len(self.theme_order)]
    240 +        self._apply_theme(next_theme)
    241 +        self._update_status()

  └ codenovel/reader.py (+42 -0)
     1 +from __future__ import annotations
     2 +
     3 +from pathlib import Path
     4 +
     5 +
     6 +PLACEHOLDER_TEXT = """
     7 +No TXT novel loaded.
     8 +
     9 +Usage:
    10 +  codenovel path\\to\\novel.txt
    11 +
    12 +Tips:
    13 +  - Keep the center pane dim so it reads like inactive terminal output.
    14 +  - Press space to pause logs before turning a page.
    15 +  - Press t to cycle between codex-like, claude-like, and opencode-like themes.
    16 +""".strip()
    17 +
    18 +
    19 +def load_book_text(book_path: Path | None) -> str:
    20 +    if book_path is None:
    21 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    22 +    if not book_path.exists():
    23 +        return f"TXT file not found:\n{book_path}"
    24 +    if book_path.suffix.lower() != ".txt":
    25 +        return f"Only .txt files are supported right now.\n\nProvided:\n{book_path.name}"
    26 +    try:
    27 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    28 +    except UnicodeDecodeError:
    29 +        return book_path.read_text(encoding="gb18030", errors="replace")
    30 +
    31 +
    32 +def style_book_text(content: str) -> str:
    33 +    lines = [line.rstrip() for line in content.splitlines()]
    34 +    if not lines:
    35 +        return PLACEHOLDER_TEXT
    36 +    styled = []
    37 +    for index, line in enumerate(lines, start=1):
    38 +        prefix = f"{index:>4} "
    39 +        safe_line = line if line else " "
    40 +        styled.append(f"{prefix}{safe_line}")
    41 +    return "\n".join(styled)
    42 +

     70 +@dataclass
     71 +class SessionContext:
     72 +    task_title: str
     73 +    seed: int
     74 +    src_count: int = 18
     75 +    test_count: int = 7
     76 +    doc_count: int = 4
     77 +    module_a: str = "terminal/theme.py"
     78 +    module_b: str = "agent/session.py"
     79 +    module_c: str = "reader/pane.py"
     80 +    file_a: str = "src/ui/session_view.tsx"
     81 +    file_b: str = "src/core/runtime.ts"
     82 +    symbol_name: str = "renderSessionState"
     83 +    test_name: str = "tests/test_session_render.py::test_dimmed_reader"
     84 +    latency: int = 34
     85 +    phase_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     86 +    bottom_cycle: cycle = field(init=False, repr=False)
     87 +
     88 +    def __post_init__(self) -> None:
     89 +        self.phase_cycle = cycle(TOP_PHASES)
     90 +        self.bottom_cycle = cycle(BOTTOM_PHASES)
     91 +
     92 +
     93 +class FakeLogEngine:
     94 +    def __init__(self, task_title: str, seed: int = 7) -> None:
     95 +        self.random = Random(seed)
     96 +        self.context = SessionContext(task_title=task_title, seed=seed)
     97 +        self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
     98 +        self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
     99 +        self.top_counter = 0
    100 +        self.bottom_counter = 0
    101 +
    102 +    def _render_template(self, template: str) -> str:
    103 +        self.context.src_count += self.random.choice((0, 1))
    104 +        self.context.test_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
    105 +        self.context.doc_count += self.random.choice((0, 0, 1))
    106 +        self.context.latency = max(12, self.context.latency + self.random.randint(-4, 7))
    107 +        return template.format(**self.context.__dict__)
    108 +
    109 +    def next_top_line(self) -> str:
    110 +        if self.top_counter and self.top_counter % 4 == 0:
    111 +            self.top_phase = next(self.context.phase_cycle)
    112 +        template = self.random.choice(TOP_TEMPLATES[self.top_phase])
    113 +        self.top_counter += 1
    114 +        return self._render_template(template)
    115 +
    116 +    def next_bottom_line(self) -> str:
    117 +        if self.bottom_counter and self.bottom_counter % 3 == 0:
    118 +            self.bottom_phase = next(self.context.bottom_cycle)
    119 +        template = self.random.choice(BOTTOM_TEMPLATES[self.bottom_phase])
    120 +        self.bottom_counter += 1
    121 +        return self._render_template(template)

  Redesigning the app interface

  I'm considering reinterpreting the novel section as the main transcript with streaming panels above and below. Perhaps a split
  transcript could work, where one dim block is fixed. Two modes make sense: a startup header and a session layout. In the session
  layout, I envision a small status line at the top saying "• Working...", with transcript items in the center. The novel might
  show in a dim output block surrounded by fake activity items. I'll also need to check if Textual can support a static header and
  footer.

  Considering the UI layout

  I'm thinking about adding a startup header if no book is loaded. However, the user might prefer a direct open fake CLI. Maybe I
  could always show a compact header box at the top with the model or directory, similar to a clear UI startup. After the
  conversation starts, the Codex layout could drop the header, which could make things simpler. A top header strip saying >_ OpenAI
  Codex (v0.1.0) could work, with the transcript below. This might make it more recognizable for the user.

  Designing app layout

  I’m thinking about creating an app layout with a static header panel at the top, maybe around five lines long, using a border
  with box characters. I’d stick to a monochrome design. The main transcript area would fill the screen and have items listed as
  lines with bullets and indentations.

  I wonder if I can have the novel displayed in a central output block styled dimly, maybe with prefixes and a faint border labeled
  "stdout". It’s a bit tricky to figure out how to keep the novel text hidden if needed. I’m considering different scroll options
  too!

  Considering tool use items

  I'm thinking about the layout for tool use items, like having "• Exploring" and a submenu for "Search...". I might include a main
  indicator like "• Working (4s • esc to interrupt)" with some fake operations followed by a dimmed block for command output, where
  the novel would fit in.

  I wonder if using Unicode bullets and box-drawing characters will be acceptable since I know the default is ASCII. I’ll need to
  update the README and consider creating a sample demo, although I might be leaning more toward replacing app.py entirely. Also, I
  need to check how to style inline dim and color with Rich Text objects.

  Creating widgets for the layout

  I'm considering creating widgets for the app. The static header panel might render text via Rich Panel, possibly using a method
  like Static update(Panel.fit(...)). For the transcript log, I think RichLog could be beneficial since it can write Text and
  Group. It likely supports the write() method with renderable types, which is great for preserving styles.

  But I’m not sure how to manage the middle novel section since it needs to stay dimmed and not change. Maybe I can seed the novel
  block into RichLog once and gradually append surrounding lines, but the user might want that novel section to scroll manually
  instead of automatically with the transcript. That's a tricky balance!

  Exploring interface design

  I'm thinking about a codex-like interface that mostly has a plain screen. I could create a reader-pane without borders and
  include a small dim label like [dim]terminal output[/dim], followed by the book text. It could resemble a tool output section. I
  also wonder about adding fake transcript lines both above and below the reader, while keeping the main text centered. This seems
  to align with my earlier ideas.

  Considering widget options

  I’m thinking about whether I could use the Input widget while it’s disabled, but that might capture typing. The simplest solution
  might be to use a TextArea. However, if the user just wants to see something visually appealing, I could still use Input with a
  placeholder and not worry about the input submission. My keybindings are j, k, space, t, and q, so I want to avoid intercepting
  keys. It might be better to stick with a Static widget. I also need to consider adding a spinner or elapsed timer line that
  updates reactively.

  Simplifying the theme options

  I’m thinking it might be best to simplify to just the Codex visual theme and remove the --theme option. Altering the CLI could be
  okay, but I want to be cautious about backward compatibility. If the user specifically asks for Codex, I should probably focus on
  that theme only. I’ll need to inspect the current app code for necessary modifications, potentially rewriting app.py
  significantly to clarify choices around --theme.

  Considering style implementation

  I'm thinking about the style for the screen background. Perhaps a transparent background could be nice? It might allow the text
  to stand out better if the text color is black. This setup could create a sleek and clean look. I'm curious whether this default
  background choice will suit all design aspects, and I want to ensure it enhances readability. Let's explore how this might come
  together!

  Considering task launch options

  The user might prefer to launch directly with just the novel. I could use --title to set a current fake task and display it first
  in the transcript. That sounds like a good idea! I need to think about whether to allow theme cycling anymore, especially since
  it’s only using codex. Instead, it might be better to repurpose t for cycling through verbosity. I’ll also consider new
  keybindings like q/space/j/k/pageup/down and plan to remove t. Updating the CLI and README is necessary.

  Considering transcript details

  I think the bottom transcript should mainly reflect the current request and any recent steps taken. It seems important to keep
  the information relevant and avoid clutter, so users can easily follow along. A clean layout with just the essentials might be
  what I need to focus on. I'll aim to make sure it captures the essence of the request without overwhelming with too much
  information. Keeping clarity in mind is key!

  Considering event templates

  I'm thinking about defining event templates for the top and bottom of a structure, and potentially using phase states. My idea is
  that next_group() could return a dictionary that includes the main element, a list of children, and designations for the top and
  bottom. This could be a useful approach for organizing data more clearly. It feels like this will make things more structured and
  manageable!

  Updating simulator structure

  I'm planning to patch the simulator. I'll create a RenderedLine dataclass with properties like kind and text, and I’m considering
  phases, including a list for commentary templates and explored search templates. For the next_top_group() function, I might
  include a commentary one-liner if the count is divisible by three, or otherwise choose an event group based on a cycle of
  actions. I want to ensure there's a distinction between top-level commentary and recent summaries in the output.

  Considering reader adjustments

  I’m thinking about labeling the output as “inactive terminal output” at the top, but the user prefers it hidden. That’s
  interesting! Maybe I should consider implementing a scroll feature for the reader. Auto-scrolling logs while keeping the reader
  independent sounds like a good idea. I might patch the reader style by adding four spaces at the start of each line. I’m
  wondering if I should leave out line numbers or manually wrap lines—probably not. Let's move on with patching reader.py!

• Edited 5 files (+587 -0)
  └ README.md (+49 -0)
     1 +# codenovel
     2 +
     3 +`codenovel` is a Codex-like fake AI coding terminal that hides TXT novel content in a dimmed center pane while synthetic tr
        anscript activity scrolls around it.
     4 +
     5 +## Install
     6 +
     7 +```bash
     8 +pip install .
     9 +```
    10 +
    11 +For development:
    12 +
    13 +```bash
    14 +pip install -e .
    15 +```
    16 +
    17 +If you open `cmd` in this project directory, you can also run:
    18 +
    19 +```bat
    20 +codenovel novel.txt
    21 +```
    22 +
    23 +The local `codenovel.bat` wrapper calls `python -m codenovel` for you.
    24 +
    25 +## Run
    26 +
    27 +```bash
    28 +codenovel path/to/novel.txt
    29 +```
    30 +
    31 +Equivalent fallback if your `pip` scripts directory is not on `PATH`:
    32 +
    33 +```bash
    34 +python -m codenovel path/to/novel.txt
    35 +```
    36 +
    37 +Optional title override:
    38 +
    39 +```bash
    40 +codenovel novel.txt --title "Summarize recent commits"
    41 +```
    42 +
    43 +## Controls
    44 +
    45 +- `j` / `Down`: scroll novel down
    46 +- `k` / `Up`: scroll novel up
    47 +- `PageDown` / `PageUp`: faster scrolling
    48 +- `space`: pause or resume fake activity
    49 +- `q`: quit

     83 +class CodeNovelApp(App[None]):
     84 +    CSS = BASE_CSS
     85 +    BINDINGS = [
     86 +        Binding("q", "quit", "Quit"),
     87 +        Binding("space", "toggle_pause", "Pause"),
     88 +        Binding("j,down", "scroll_down", "Down"),
     89 +        Binding("k,up", "scroll_up", "Up"),
     90 +        Binding("pagedown", "page_down", "Page Down"),
     91 +        Binding("pageup", "page_up", "Page Up"),
     92 +    ]
     93 +
     94 +    paused = reactive(False)
     95 +
     96 +    def __init__(self, book_path: Path | None, task_title: str) -> None:
     97 +        super().__init__()
     98 +        self.book_path = book_path
     99 +        self.task_title = task_title
    100 +        self.engine = FakeLogEngine(task_title=task_title, seed=randint(1, 999_999))
    101 +        self.started_at = monotonic()
    102 +
    103 +    def compose(self) -> ComposeResult:
    104 +        yield Container(
    105 +            Static(id="header"),
    106 +            RichLog(id="top-log", wrap=True, highlight=False, markup=False),
    107 +            Static(id="reader-label"),
    108 +            VerticalScroll(
    109 +                Static(id="reader-text"),
    110 +                id="reader-scroll",
    111 +            ),
    112 +            RichLog(id="recent-log", wrap=True, highlight=False, markup=False),
    113 +            Static(id="working-line"),
    114 +            Static(id="composer"),
    115 +            Static(id="footer"),
    116 +            id="root",
    117 +        )
    118 +
    119 +    def on_mount(self) -> None:
    120 +        self._render_header()
    121 +        self._load_book()
    122 +        self._render_reader_label()
    123 +        self._render_composer()
    124 +        self._render_footer()
    125 +        self._seed_logs()
    126 +        self._update_working_line()
    127 +        self.set_interval(0.85, self._tick_top)
    128 +        self.set_interval(1.35, self._tick_bottom)
    129 +        self.set_interval(1.0, self._tick_clock)
    130 +
    131 +    def _render_header(self) -> None:
    132 +        model_line = Text()
    133 +        model_line.append("model:     ")
    134 +        model_line.append("gpt-5-codex", style="magenta")
    135 +        model_line.append(" high   ")
    136 +        model_line.append("/model to change", style="dim")
    137 +
    138 +        directory_line = Text()
    139 +        directory_line.append("directory: ")
    140 +        directory_line.append(str(Path.cwd()), style="dim")
    141 +
    142 +        title = Text()
    143 +        title.append(">_ ", style="cyan")
    144 +        title.append("OpenAI Codex", style="bold")
    145 +        title.append(f" (v{__version__})", style="dim")
    146 +
    147 +        header = Text()
    148 +        header.append_text(title)
    149 +        header.append("\n\n")
    150 +        header.append_text(model_line)
    151 +        header.append("\n")
    152 +        header.append_text(directory_line)
    153 +
    154 +        self.query_one("#header", Static).update(Panel.fit(header, border_style="white"))
    155 +
    156 +    def _load_book(self) -> None:
    157 +        book = load_book_text(self.book_path)
    158 +        self.query_one("#reader-text", Static).update(style_book_text(book))
    159 +
    160 +    def _render_reader_label(self) -> None:
    161 +        self.query_one("#reader-label", Static).update(
    162 +            Text("  inactive terminal output", style="dim")
    163 +        )
    164 +
    165 +    def _render_composer(self) -> None:
    166 +        composer = Text()
    167 +        composer.append("\n")
    168 +        composer.append("› ", style="magenta")
    169 +        composer.append("Ask Codex to do anything")
    170 +        composer.append("\n")
    171 +        self.query_one("#composer", Static).update(composer)
    172 +
    173 +    def _render_footer(self) -> None:
    174 +        width = max(self.size.width - 38, 1)
    175 +        footer = Text()
    176 +        footer.append("  ")
    177 +        footer.append("?", style="cyan")
    178 +        footer.append(" for shortcuts", style="dim")
    179 +        footer.append(" " * width)
    180 +        footer.append("100% context left", style="dim")
    181 +        self.query_one("#footer", Static).update(footer)
    182 +
    183 +    def _seed_logs(self) -> None:
    184 +        top = self.query_one("#top-log", RichLog)
    185 +        recent = self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog)
    186 +        recent.write(self._render_user_prompt(self.engine.initial_prompt()))
    187 +        for _ in range(5):
    188 +            self._write_group(top, self.engine.next_top_group())
    189 +        for _ in range(2):
    190 +            self._write_group(recent, self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    191 +
    192 +    def _tick_top(self) -> None:
    193 +        if self.paused:
    194 +            return
    195 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#top-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_top_group())
    196 +        self._update_working_line()
    197 +
    198 +    def _tick_bottom(self) -> None:
    199 +        if self.paused:
    200 +            return
    201 +        self._write_group(self.query_one("#recent-log", RichLog), self.engine.next_bottom_group())
    202 +        self._update_working_line()
    203 +
    204 +    def _tick_clock(self) -> None:
    205 +        self._update_working_line()
    206 +        self._render_footer()
    207 +
    208 +    def _update_working_line(self) -> None:
    209 +        elapsed = int(monotonic() - self.started_at)
    210 +        line = Text()
    211 +        line.append("• ", style="magenta")
    212 +        line.append(self.engine.working_status(elapsed, self.paused))
    213 +        self.query_one("#working-line", Static).update(line)
    214 +
    215 +    def _write_group(self, widget: RichLog, lines: list[RenderedLine]) -> None:
    216 +        for line in lines:
    217 +            widget.write(self._render_line(line))
    218 +
    219 +    def _render_user_prompt(self, prompt: str) -> Text:
    220 +        line = Text()
    221 +        line.append("› ", style="magenta")
    222 +        line.append(prompt)
    223 +        return line
    224 +
    225 +    def _render_line(self, line: RenderedLine) -> Text:
    226 +        text = Text()
    227 +        if line.kind == "commentary":
    228 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    229 +            text.append(line.text)
    230 +        elif line.kind == "event":
    231 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    232 +            text.append(line.text)
    233 +        elif line.kind == "child":
    234 +            text.append("  └ ", style="dim")
    235 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    236 +        elif line.kind == "child_deep":
    237 +            text.append("    ")
    238 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    239 +        elif line.kind == "command":
    240 +            text.append("  ")
    241 +            text.append(line.text, style="cyan")
    242 +        elif line.kind == "success":
    243 +            text.append("    ")
    244 +            text.append(line.text, style="green")
    245 +        elif line.kind == "queue":
    246 +            text.append("  → ", style="dim")
    247 +            text.append(line.text)
    248 +        elif line.kind == "summary":
    249 +            text.append("• ", style="magenta")
    250 +            text.append(line.text, style="dim")
    251 +        else:
    252 +            text.append(line.text)
    253 +        return text
    254 +
    255 +    def action_toggle_pause(self) -> None:
    256 +        self.paused = not self.paused
    257 +        self._update_working_line()
    258 +
    259 +    def action_scroll_down(self) -> None:
    260 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_down(animate=False)
    261 +
    262 +    def action_scroll_up(self) -> None:
    263 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_up(animate=False)
    264 +
    265 +    def action_page_down(self) -> None:
    266 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_down(animate=False)
    267 +
    268 +    def action_page_up(self) -> None:
    269 +        self.query_one("#reader-scroll", VerticalScroll).scroll_page_up(animate=False)
